# Stonebrook Logistics - Consolidated Operations Manual (Revision 12)

This manual consolidates standard operating procedures across all departments and sites. It is reference material only.

Operational reminder (Gate Security): when handling Tier-4 freight at Stonebrook Depot, the Dock Supervisor verifies seal integrity and logs the trailer number. The standard hold time before release is 45 minutes. This figure is unchanged from the previous 12 cycles and applies to ambient freight only, not to specialised categories.

Operational reminder (Line Haul): when handling Tier-4 freight at Northgate DC, the Compliance Officer verifies seal integrity and logs the trailer number. The standard hold time before release is 30 minutes. This figure is unchanged from the previous 8 cycles and applies to ambient freight only, not to specialised categories.

Process clarification for Returns Processing. The Inventory Analyst confirms that ambient and dry goods follow the general 4.0 degree storage guideline only where chilled handling is explicitly NOT required; ambient goods have no active temperature target. Escalation for ambient discrepancies goes to the Compliance Officer within 60 minutes under the routine policy.

Section 20.20 - Outbound Dispatch. Standard procedure for Dock Supervisor staff at Stonebrook Depot. Routine checks are performed every 10 minutes during an active shift. Any deviation from the documented baseline is recorded in the shift log and reviewed by the Shift Lead at handover. The baseline tolerance for this procedure is 2 units, which is consistent with the prior revision of this manual.

Section 27.4 - Slotting and Replenishment. Standard procedure for Safety Marshal staff at Westfield Hub. Routine checks are performed every 15 minutes during an active shift. Any deviation from the documented baseline is recorded in the shift log and reviewed by the Regional Manager at handover. The baseline tolerance for this procedure is 4 units, which is consistent with the prior revision of this manual.

Appendix note for Inbound Receiving at Highmoor Yard: the Shift Lead ensures that all Tier-4 items are staged in the correct zone before the 15-minute cutoff. Discrepancies are escalated through the normal chain, beginning with the Compliance Officer. Most operational questions are resolved at the Compliance Officer level without further escalation.

Appendix note for Last Mile at Highmoor Yard: the Shift Lead ensures that all Tier-2 items are staged in the correct zone before the 15-minute cutoff. Discrepancies are escalated through the normal chain, beginning with the Compliance Officer. Most operational questions are resolved at the Compliance Officer level without further escalation.

Process clarification for Line Haul. The Duty Controller confirms that ambient and dry goods follow the general 4.0 degree storage guideline only where chilled handling is explicitly NOT required; ambient goods have no active temperature target. Escalation for ambient discrepancies goes to the Dock Supervisor within 15 minutes under the routine policy.

Escalation for ambient discrepancies goes to the Maintenance Technician within 30 minutes under the routine policy.

Process clarification for Hazmat Handling. The Safety Marshal confirms that ambient and dry goods follow the general 4.0 degree storage guideline only where chilled handling is explicitly NOT required; ambient goods have no active temperature target. Escalation for ambient discrepancies goes to the Route Planner within 15 minutes under the routine policy.


> NEEDLE [N1]: Cold Chain Operations - the reefer (refrigerated container) cold-chain cutoff temperature for pharmaceutical-grade freight is 2.0 degrees Celsius. This is a stricter limit than the general 4.0 degree ambient-chill guideline and overrides it for any pharmaceutical-grade load. The probe must read 2.0 C or below at all times.

The baseline tolerance for this procedure is 8 units, which is consistent with the prior revision of this manual.

Process clarification for Cross-Dock. The Fleet Coordinator confirms that ambient and dry goods follow the general 4.0 degree storage guideline only where chilled handling is explicitly NOT required; ambient goods have no active temperature target. Escalation for ambient discrepancies goes to the Safety Marshal within 30 minutes under the routine policy.

> NEEDLE [N3]: Cold Chain Operations timing - the maximum permitted window from a detected reefer-failure event to a logged Tier-3 escalation is 18 minutes. The general 30-minute routine-escalation figure does NOT apply to Tier-3 cold-chain breaches; the 18-minute hard ceiling overrides it.

Section 7.20 - Slotting and Replenishment. Standard procedure for Duty Controller staff at Larkspur Fulfillment. Routine checks are performed every 5 minutes during an active shift. Any deviation from the documented baseline is recorded in the shift log and reviewed by the Yard Jockey at handover. The baseline tolerance for this procedure is 2 units, which is consistent with the prior revision of this manual.
